name:I‚ÄçR‚ÄçF‚ÄçA‚ÄçN‚Äç ‚ÄçH‚ÄçA‚ÄçN‚ÄçI‚ÄçF
info:Premier Lakeview Kingsize Room

info:Solo travelers
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted October 17, 2021
msg:After an initial hiccup with the first hotel booking, Trip.com customer service helped me to find another hotel close to the first one. Marriott Hotel Wuxi Luneng was that one. And it really helped to recover what had been a not too good start to my weekend in Wuxi. I stayed in a Premier Lakeside King-size room. As the name suggests it has a balcony giving a great view of the Yuantouzhu scenic park and Lake Taihu. The room itself is best described by photos and I will save me typing too much. I had the breakfast which has a lot of choice and if you have time you can relax in there for a while and make it a brunch. There is a 7x24 gym on the B1 level, a swimming pool and sauna too. All in all I recommend this as a good hotel to stay for a long weekend to see Yuantouzhu scenic park (only a five minute taxi drive away) and other areas of Wuxi.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Executive Lakeview Double Beds Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:The whole family traveled and booked a lake view executive twin room and an executive twin room.
Let's talk about the geographical location first. It is on the shore of Lihu Lake. The distance across the road from the hotel is Lihu Lake. Many people camp and set up tents on the grass. Liyuan and Lihu Park are close at hand. It takes 13 minutes to ride a bike from Yuantouzhu, half an hour to walk, and run around Lihu Lake for 10 km. It is very beautiful and very suitable for a leisurely parent-child vacation.
Regarding the service, my personal experience is that I think the service is very good! First of all, whether it is the doorman picking up the luggage or opening and closing the car door, they are very proactive. They are also patient and polite when waiting for a table or consulting in the restaurant, and the room service is also timely. The best is the front desk LULU, who is beautiful, kind and very professional. For the extended stay, the room was upgraded to an executive lake view room. When she learned that she would leave at 6 pm the next day, she took the initiative to delay the check-out to 4 pm. It was really very meticulous and considerate, making people feel at home! The hardware of the hotel can be copied, but the service is a soft competitive advantage. Just based on this service based on customer experience, I will choose Luneng Marriott again!
Let's talk about the room. I checked for a long time before the trip, and finally chose Luneng Marriott Hotel. The main reason is that the single bed in the hotel's twin room is 1.4 meters wide. I don't know why there are relatively few parent-child rooms in five-star hotels in Wuxi. For families like me who go out with big children, a single bed with enough width can basically meet the needs. It's not crowded for three people to sleep in one room. In addition, let's talk about the executive room. First, the floor is high, on the 9th floor. 8th and below are non-executive rooms. The view is better on the higher floors. In addition, the exclusive executive lounge has snacks, drinks and light meals. If the dinner requirements are not high, the light meals in the executive lounge can fully meet them.
The hotel's breakfast is relatively rich, with many varieties and good taste, but there are also many people on holidays, and there is always a queue in the area where wonton noodles are made.

msg:Are all Marriott services like this? Is it worthy of Luneng‚Äôs brand?
    From check-in to check-out, no one from the staff reminded me why I paid twice to book 4 rooms. It's not that the hotel is at fault, it's just that I was drunk and somehow spent 4 cents to book 4 identical rooms. As a result, the other three hotels did not open rooms but only deducted payment. Afterwards, I found that no matter how much communication was done, it was useless.
    Can you only blame yourself for drinking too much? Or did the password-free payment on the APP help me book 3 more rooms? But the hotel has an attitude that it has nothing to do with it. Is it following the rules, or is it disappointing the guests?
